The Mirage Flame Panel creates a see-through view of the flames straight to the back of the box with ThruView Full-depth design.\u00a0Partially frosted acrylic panel is clearly better than a mirror, showing only dazzling flames and no reflections. Adjust the flame base color to red or blue and customize the firebox glow with a choice of warm hues, plus midnight mode. You can also adjust\u00a0light level to suit your room and choose flicker effect for enhanced firelight. Installed\u00a0Ambient Light Sensor automatically adjusts firebox light to suit\u00a0the room day to night.\u00a0Adjust the flames, lighting and heat with an included smart remote.\u00a0Dimplex Revillusion\u00a036 inch Built-In Electric Firebox comes with front glass panel & plug in kit. It can be installed with front glass panel or open face. This enhances the traditional masonry\u00a0open look of the fireplace. Designed to be direct-wired to a 120, 208 or 220/240 volt circuit for a seamless look (optional plug kit available). The Powerful heater can put out from 4400 BTUs (120v) up to 8794 BTU's (220/240V). It produces quick and lasting heat for rooms up to 400 sqft (if wired to 120V) or up to 800 sqft (if wired to 220/240V).
